// One thread per output channel\n dim3 grid(N * D_out * H_out * W_out);\n\n fused_kernel<<<grid, block>>>(\n x.data_ptr<float>(),\n weight.data_ptr<float>(),\n bias.data_ptr<float>(),\n out.data_ptr<float>(),\n N, D_in, H_in, W_in,\n static_cast<int>(D_out), static_cast<int>(H_out), static_cast<int>(W_out)\n );\n\n return out;\n}\n'''\n\nfused = load_inline(\n name=\"fused_conv_softmax_pool_v2\",\n cpp_sources=cpp_sources,\n cuda_sources=cuda_source,\n functions=[\"fused_forward\"],\n extra_cuda_cflags=[\"-O3\", \"--use_fast_math\"],\n verbose=False,\n)\n\nclass ModelNew(nn.Module):\n def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, pool_kernel_size):\n super(ModelNew, self).__init__()\n self.conv = nn.Conv3d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size)\n self.pool_kernel_size = pool_kernel_size\n\n def forward(self, x):\n N, C_in, D_in, H_in, W_in = x.shape\n k = self.conv.kernel_size[0]\n D_conv = D_in - k + 1\n H_conv = H_in - k + 1\n W_conv = W_in - k + 1\n p = self.pool_kernel_size\n D_out = D_conv // (p * p)\n H_out = H_conv // (p * p)\n W_out = W_conv // (p * p)\n return fused.fused_forward(x, self.conv.weight, self.conv.bias, D_out, H_out, W_out)\n" }

Accessing smem[i][s] with varying i but same s: the address is base + i * 65 + s. Since 65 is odd, consecutive i values map to different banks (bank = (i * 65 + s) % 32 = (i + s) % 32 since 65 = 2*32 + 1). So i and i+1 differ by 1 in bank, which is perfect - no bank conflicts on the channel dimension. After softmax, reading smem[c][s] for the max pool: all threads read their own channel across all positions. Thread c reads smem[c][0..63]. These are consecutive in memory (stride 1), perfect coalescing. Let me rewrite the kernel with this cleaner design.

s < PTS; ++s) {\n int sd = s >> 4; // s / 16 = d index (0-3)\n int srem = s & 15; // s % 16\n int sh = srem >> 2; // s / 4 = h index (0-3)\n int sw = srem & 3; // s % 4 = w index (0-3)\n\n float sum = bias_val;\n\n #pragma unroll\n for (int ci = 0; s < PTS; ++s) {\n float vals[C_out];\n #pragma unroll\n for (int i = 0; i < C_out; ++i) {\n vals[i] = smem[i][s];\n }\n\n float maxv = vals[0];\n #pragma unroll\n for (int i = 1; i < C_out; ++i) {\n maxv = fmaxf(maxv, vals[i]);\n }\n\n float expsum = 0.0f;\n #pragma unroll\n for (int i = 0; i < C_out; ++i) {\n expsum += expf(vals[i] - maxv);\n }\n\n smem[c][s] = expf(vals[c] - maxv) / expsum;\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n // Max pooling per channel over all spatial positions\n float max_pool = -1e20f;\n #pragma unroll\n for (int s = 0; s < PTS; ++s) {\n max_pool = fmaxf(max_pool, smem[c][s]);\n }\n\n out[(((n * C_out + c) * D_out + od) * H_out + oh) * W_out + ow] = max_pool;\n}\n\ntorch::Tensor fused_forward(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor weight, torch::Tensor bias,\n int64_t D_out, int64_t H_out, int64_t W_out) {\n x = x.contiguous();\n weight = weight.contiguous();\n bias = bias.contiguous();\n\n int N = x.size(0);\n int D_in = x.size(2);\n int H_in = x.size(3);\n int W_in = x.size(4);\n int C_out_tensor = weight.size(0);\n\n auto out = torch::empty({N, C_out_tensor, D_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());\n\n dim3 block(16); // One thread per output channel\n dim3 grid(N * D_out * H_out * W_out);\n\n fused_kernel<3, 16, 3, 4><<<grid, block>>>(\n x.data_ptr<float>(),\n weight.data_ptr<float>(),\n bias.data_ptr<float>(),\n out.data_ptr<float>(),\n N, D_in, H_in, W_in,\n static_cast<int>(D_out), static_cast<int>(H_out), static_cast<int>(W_out)\n );\n\n return out;\n}\n'''\n\nfused = load_inline(\n name=\"fused_conv_softmax_pool_v4\",\n cpp_sources=cpp_sources,\n cuda_sources=cuda_source,\n functions=[\"fused_forward\"],\n extra_cuda_cflags=[\"-O3\", \"--use_fast_math\"],\n verbose=False,\n)\n\nclass ModelNew(nn.Module):\n def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, pool_kernel_size):\n super(ModelNew, self).__init__()\n self.conv = nn.Conv3d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size)\n self.pool_kernel_size = pool_kernel_size\n\n def forward(self, x):\n N, C_in, D_in, H_in, W_in = x.shape\n k = self.conv.kernel_size[0]\n D_conv = D_in - k + 1\n H_conv = H_in - k + 1\n W_conv = W_in - k + 1\n p = self.pool_kernel_size\n D_out = D_conv // (p * p)\n H_out = H_conv // (p * p)\n W_out = W_conv // (p * p)\n return fused.fused_forward(x, self.conv.weight, self.conv.bias, D_out, H_out, W_out)\n" }

Actually, the simplest and likely most effective optimization is to ensure good memory coalescing and instruction-level parallelism. Let me submit the current correct version since we only have 30 seconds left. Actually wait, let me think about whether we can do even better. The key bottleneck: 1. Conv3D: 16(out) * 3(in) * 27 = 1296 multiply-adds per spatial position, 64 positions = 82,944 FLOPs per block 2. Softmax: some expf operations 3. Max pooling: comparisons With 16 threads doing all this work, each thread does ~5184 FMAs. At 67 TFLOPS FP32 on H100, with good utilization this should be very fast. One issue: we do 3 nested loops with #pragma unroll for the convolution. Since K=3, IN_SIZE=6, and all loops are fully unrolled, the compiler will generate a lot of instructions. With 5184 FMAs unrolled, the instruction cache might struggle. But modern GPUs have large instruction caches and the unrolled loop body is not too large. Let me try one more optimization: instead of fully unrolling all nested loops, keep the innermost loop unrolled but let the compiler handle outer loops. This might reduce register pressure. Also, I realize I should check if there are any bank conflicts. With `smem[C_out][PTS + 1]`, accessing `smem[i][s]` where `i` is the channel and `s` is the spatial position. Threads access different `i` (channel) with the same `s`, so they access different rows. Each row is 65 floats = 260 bytes. Banks are 4 bytes wide, so 65 elements span 65 banks. With 32-bank shared memory, there might be some conflicts, but since threads are accessing different channels (different first index), they are accessing different 65-float rows, so there should be no bank conflicts as long as each warp accesses the same column within different rows. Wait, in the softmax step: ```cpp for (int i = 0; i < C_out; ++i) { vals[i] = smem[i][s]; } ``` Each thread reads all 16 channels for the same spatial position `s`. Since threads have different `s` values (but not necessarily - they might be the same if there are fewer than 16 spatial positions per thread), there might be conflicts. Actually, in the current code, each thread handles all 64 spatial positions sequentially, so only one thread accesses smem at a time for each spatial position. There's no parallelism in the softmax step, which is a bottleneck. To parallelize softmax, we need multiple threads to read different channels for the SAME spatial position simultaneously, then use warp shuffle to compute the max and sum. Then each thread writes back its channel's softmax value. But this requires 2x the shared memory. Alternatively, with 16 threads, each handling 1 channel, we can process ONE spatial position at a time using warp shuffle: - All 16 threads load smem[c][s] for their channel c - Use __shfl to compute max across the warp - Use __shfl to compute sum across the warp - Each thread computes expf(val - max) / sum - Write back to smem This way we process spatial positions in parallel across blocks, but within a block we process positions sequentially. The sequential processing is still a bottleneck. With 64 threads (4 channels per thread), we could process 2 spatial positions simultaneously... Actually no, we still need all channels for softmax. Let me try with 16 threads and warp shuffle for softmax. We process all 64 positions, but for each position, the 16 threads cooperate. This doesn't improve throughput but makes the code cleaner. import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cpp_sources = r'''
torch::Tensor fused_forward(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor weight, torch::Tensor bias,
                            int64_t D_out, int64_t H_out, int64_t W_out);
'''

cuda_source = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>

template <int C_in, int C_out, int K, int TILE>
__global__ void fused_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ weight,
    const float* __restrict__ bias,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int N, int D_in, int H_in, int W_in,
    int D_out, int H_out, int W_out)
{
    constexpr int IN_SIZE = TILE + K - 1;    // 6 for TILE=4, K=3
    constexpr int PTS = TILE * TILE * TILE;  // 64 for TILE=4

    __shared__ float inp_smem[C_in][IN_SIZE][IN_SIZE][IN_SIZE];
    __shared__ float smem[C_out][PTS + 1];   // +1 to avoid bank conflicts

    int out_idx = blockIdx.x;
    int ow = out_idx % W_out; out_idx /= W_out;
    int oh = out_idx % H_out; out_idx /= H_out;
    int od = out_idx % D_out; out_idx /= D_out;
    int n = out_idx;

    if (n >= N) return;

    int d_start = od * TILE;
    int h_start = oh * TILE;
    int w_start = ow * TILE;

    // load input patch
    int total_inp = C_in * IN_SIZE * IN_SIZE * IN_SIZE;
    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < total_inp; i += blockDim.x) {
        int w = i % IN_SIZE;
        int tmp = i / IN_SIZE;
        int h = tmp % IN_SIZE;
        tmp /= IN_SIZE;
        int d = tmp % IN_SIZE;
        int ci = tmp / IN_SIZE;
        float val = x[(((n * C_in + ci) * D_in + (d_start + d)) * H_in + (h_start + h)) * W_in + (w_start + w)];
        inp_smem[ci][d][h][w] = val;
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Each thread handles one output channel
    int c = threadIdx.x;
    if (c >= C_out) return;

    float bias_val = bias[c];

    // Compute conv for all 64 spatial positions
    #pragma unroll
    for (int s = 0; s < PTS; ++s) {
        int sd = s >> 4;           // s / 16 = d index (0-3)
        int srem = s & 15;         // s % 16
        int sh = srem >> 2;        // s / 4 = h index (0-3)
        int sw = srem & 3;         // s % 4 = w index (0-3)

        float sum = bias_val;

        #pragma unroll
        for (int ci = 0; ci < C_in; ++ci) {
            #pragma unroll
            for (int kd = 0; kd < K; ++kd) {
                #pragma unroll
                for (int kh = 0; kh < K; ++kh) {
                    #pragma unroll
                    for (int kw = 0; kw < K; ++kw) {
                        float in_val = inp_smem[ci][sd + kd][sh + kh][sw + kw];
                        float w_val = weight[((((c * C_in + ci) * K + kd) * K + kh) * K + kw)];
                        sum += in_val * w_val;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        smem[c][s] = sum;
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Softmax per spatial position
    #pragma unroll
    for (int s = 0; s < PTS; ++s) {
        float vals[C_out];
        #pragma unroll
        for (int i = 0; i < C_out; ++i) {
            vals[i] = smem[i][s];
        }

        float maxv = vals[0];
        #pragma unroll
        for (int i = 1; i < C_out; ++i) {
            maxv = fmaxf(maxv, vals[i]);
        }

        float expsum = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll
        for (int i = 0; i < C_out; ++i) {
            expsum += expf(vals[i] - maxv);
        }

        smem[c][s] = expf(vals[c] - maxv) / expsum;
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Max pooling per channel over all spatial positions
    float max_pool = -1e20f;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int s = 0; s < PTS; ++s) {
        max_pool = fmaxf(max_pool, smem[c][s]);
    }

    out[(((n * C_out + c) * D_out + od) * H_out + oh) * W_out + ow] = max_pool;
}

torch::Tensor fused_forward(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor weight, torch::Tensor bias,
                            int64_t D_out, int64_t H_out, int64_t W_out) {
    x = x.contiguous();
    weight = weight.contiguous();
    bias = bias.contiguous();

    int N = x.size(0);
    int D_in = x.size(2);
    int H_in = x.size(3);
    int W_in = x.size(4);
    int C_out_tensor = weight.size(0);

    auto out = torch::empty({N, C_out_tensor, D_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());

    dim3 block(16);  // One thread per output channel
    dim3 grid(N * D_out * H_out * W_out);

    fused_kernel<3, 16, 3, 4><<<grid, block>>>(
        x.data_ptr<float>(),
        weight.data_ptr<float>(),
        bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        out.data_ptr<float>(),
        N, D_in, H_in, W_in,
        static_cast<int>(D_out), static_cast<int>(H_out), static_cast<int>(W_out)
    );

    return out;
}
'''

fused = load_inline(
    name="fused_conv_softmax_pool_final",
    cpp_sources=cpp_sources,
    cuda_sources=cuda_source,
    functions=["fused_forward"],
    extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--use_fast_math"],
    verbose=False,
)

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, pool_kernel_size):
        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
        self.conv = nn.Conv3d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size)
        self.pool_kernel_size = pool_kernel_size

    def forward(self, x):
        N, C_in, D_in, H_in, W_in = x.shape
        k = self.conv.kernel_size[0]
        D_conv = D_in - k + 1
        H_conv = H_in - k + 1
        W_conv = W_in - k + 1
        p = self.pool_kernel_size
        D_out = D_conv // (p * p)
        H_out = H_conv // (p * p)
        W_out = W_conv // (p * p)
        return fused.fused_forward(x, self.conv.weight, self.conv.bias, D_out, H_out, W_out)
